Much love,  An American who survived two viruses...Trump then Covid.... and just barely.

This is brilliant. One of the best videos I have seen in 2021
Honestly I would have liked the fireworks display without the music, sound effects and narration. Think whatever you will about the message, but some things are just better when you can bask in the glow of it. Fireworks, a nice fire, a volcanic eruption, all these things are wondrous on there own without pop music and cheesy messages playing over them. It just gets distracting. As for the drones, the choreography is mind blowing and certainly a feat of modern technology, but I would have left them out altogether. The reason for the narration is because without it, the images of the drones without context would be confusing - a doctor, a sea turtle, etc. But because I feel like the narration was just distracting, I would have either done something else with the drones or just removed them altogether. Drones are great for light shows, but I think it's more difficult fitting them into a fireworks show because they are two different mediums. Part of the fun of fireworks is that they're only a temporary flash of light followed by a terrific bang. Drones in contrast are small, can stay on for extended periods of time and don't make much noise. That's why I think drones, like lasers and other electronic devices are better put with music, narration and choreography to give them context. Fireworks don't usually need an explanation. Even in the times I've seen fireworks added to music it was usually done in a way where the fireworks themselves were like an instrument. This display felt more like the music and fireworks were fighting against each other.

WISHING YOU A HAPPIEST PROSPEROUS 2021 NEW YEAR AROUND THE WORLD   Fireworks Exploded Over Empty Streets; Muted Celebrations Across Globe Blue and gold fireworks sparked into the skies of the world's largest cities as every year. The lions of London's Trafalgar Square were barricaded off, as Red Square in Moscow and Madrid's Puerta del Sol. Good riddance, 2020, Hello,2021. Some cities planned,like Sydney, to launch fireworks over empty streets. Others, such as London and Singapore,just called their displays off. Paris,Rome and Istanbul were under curfew. The New Year's Eve countdown ball was set to drop on Broadway. But in place of thousands of New Yorkers jammed shoulder to shoulder in Times Square, the audience would be a pre-selected group of nurses,doctors and other key workers,kept six feet apart in socially distanced pens. With more than 1.7 millions people dead and 82 million infected around the globe since last New Year's Eve -- yet hope that vaccines can help tame the pandemic-- the year ended unlike any other in memory.  Angela Merkel,in her 16th New Year's Eve address as German Chancellor,said as much. " Never in the last 15 years have we found the old year so heavy. And never have we, despite all the worries and some scepticism,looked forward to the new one with so much hope,"  Germany banned the sale of firework  In Australia,where Sydney's fireworks annually serve as the world's first big visual display of the New Year gatherings were banned and internal borders were shut.Most people were barred from Sydney's downtown.Famous nights spots were eerily deserted." What a hell of a year it's been". said Gladys Berrjiklian,premier of New South Wales state,which includes Sydney. "Hopefully the 2021 will be easier on all of us". In South Korea, Seoul cancelled it's New Year's Eve bell ringing ceremony in the Jongno neighbourhood for the first time since the event was first held in 1953,months after the end of the Korean War.  New Zealand held usual New Year's actuvities.Taiwan also hosted it's usual New Year's celebration, a fireworks display by its capital iconic Taipei 101 tower.  Much of Japan welcomed 2021 quietly at home. In Britain under  ever tighter restrictions to fight a more contentious virus variant,official billboards instruct  the people to " see in the New Year safely at home". In France,night curfew was in force. But there were celebrations -- small but with style". " I stuffed myself with foie grass and champagne," a Parisian said. " And stayed at home."
